ArcFlow AI Enabled Cloud ERP Training & Support
Welcome to the ArcFlow ERP Training Guide. This comprehensive manual is crafted to provide you with the essential knowledge and skills to effectively use the ArcFlow ERP system. It includes detailed walkthrough documents and instructional videos on each module, as well as insights into the workflow dependencies between modules.
Whether you are new to ERP systems or seeking to deepen your expertise in ArcFlow's advanced features, this guide will lead you through each module, showing you how to streamline business processes, enhance productivity, and achieve seamless integration across all departments. Join us on this journey to master the tools and functionalities that will propel your organisations success.
￼
Self Paced Training Guides
The training guide is organised into the various ArcFlow modules to facilitate easy navigation. Please select the dropdown menu to view the different sub-modules available. Once you have chosen a specific sub-module, you will be able to access detailed videos and comprehensive walkthrough documentation tailored to that sub-module, ensuring you have all the resources needed to master each aspect of the ArcFlow system. You can utilise the search bar at the top right of your screen to find specific training content.

	•	ArcFlow Workflow and Module Dependancy
	•	High Level ArcFlow Workflow Overview
	•	The descriptions and diagram below illustrate the workflows that the system uses to support your daily manufacturing operations. Each workflow occurs within the listed modules, and once a workflow is completed within one module, it seamlessly transitions to the next module in the process.
	•	The description outlines the entire process, starting from loading products, assemblies, and items onto the system and creating their manufacturing routes. With these routes established, you can create sales orders and production orders, as well as initiate the ordering of necessary stock.
	•	After production orders are completed, the process outlines the steps from fulfillment to customer delivery, ensuring a smooth transition from production to final delivery.
	•	High Level ArcFlow Workflow Process
	•	Process 1: Blueprints and Routing
	•	You will begin by loading your items, assemblies, and products onto the system. After this, you will create the Bill of Materials (BOM) structures for these assemblies and products. Next, you can add stock values into your warehouse, which will integrate with the production and ordering processes.
	•	Once the BOM structures are in place, you can establish the manufacturing routes for the assemblies and products. With these routes created, you can then develop production plans for the assemblies and routes.
	•	Finally, after these steps are completed, you can add the sellable items, assemblies, and products to sales quotes and create sales orders.
	•	Process 2: Customers and Sales Orders
	•	You can quote customers and create sales orders for sellable items, assemblies, and products from your blueprints library. Once a customer accepts a quote, you can generate a sales order, which is then transferred to the production team via the manufacturing module to develop a production plan.
	•	Process 3: Production Orders
	•	You can now create production orders to fulfill your sales order. The system will calculate any stock shortfalls and notify the procurement department to create an order plan for the required raw materials. If sufficient stock or finished sellable items are available, the system will account for this accordingly.
	•	Process 4: Suppliers and Order Plans
	•	The procurement department will be notified of the production order and provided with a list of items needed to complete the production plan. You will then create a Request for Quote (RFQ) with multiple suppliers. Once a supplier's quote is accepted, a purchase order will be generated. You will track the receipt of the orders and generate a Goods Received Note to capture the received stock.
	•	Process 5: Warehousing
	•	Once a Goods Received Note has been created, you can assign the ordered items to various warehouse areas, such as raw materials.
	•	When the stock is available, you can initiate production plans and start allocating jobs, beginning with the kitting process.
	•	The warehouse also functions as temporary storage for completed sub-assemblies during their routing process, as well as a holding area for final goods awaiting customer delivery.
	•	Process 6: Work Orders, Job Cards, Kitting and Production Routes
	•	Work Orders are generated from production plans to schedule the start date, contents, and quantities of production.
	•	Subsequently, job cards are created to commence the production process based on the routing of assemblies and products established in the blueprints module.
	•	The first step in the routing of assemblies or products is to kit the necessary items for the assembly route or assemble the products for the final route.
	•	Job cards are associated with the processes involved in converting raw materials into assemblies and final products.
	•	These job cards are then allocated to employees responsible for carrying out and completing the processes at designated workstations along your production line.
	•	Upon completion of the final route, the products are stored in either the final goods storage or assembly storage in preparation for customer delivery.
	•	Process 7: Storage for Customer Delivery
	•	Once the products are completed, they are stored in their final goods storage unit. Upon availability, the fulfilment team is notified to commence the picking, packing, and scheduling of delivery to fulfil the sales order.
	•	Process 8: Order Fulfilment and Delivery
	•	The fulfillment team will proceed to generate a picking list containing the items required for delivery. Once the picking process is complete, you will package the contents and affix the appropriate labels.
	•	Following packaging, the goods will be temporarily stored in a designated area, ready for either customer pickup or collection by the courier supplier for delivery to the customer.
	•	You can track the delivery progress using waybills to ensure successful delivery.
	•	High Level ArcFlow Workflow Diagram and Module Dependancy
System Configuration Overview
System Configuration Module Description:
The "System Configuration" module encompasses essential functionalities tailored to set up and customize system parameters.
You are able to setup your company information which feeds into customer, supplier and GRN documentation for recording and accounting keeping.
Tax rules and regulations allow you to create different tax classes to be assigned to sellable items, assemblies and products. The tax class are assigned to these sellable types to different customers for different tax jurisdictions during the quoting and invoicing stages.
System Configuration Process Flow:
￼
System Configuration Sub Modules:
	•	Tax Rules and Regulations
This component provides tools for configuring tax-related parameters, including tax rates, jurisdictions, exemptions, and compliance requirements. Users can define tax rules based on regional regulations, product categories, or customer attributes, ensuring accurate calculation and application of taxes across transactions. Additionally, this functionality supports updates to tax laws and regulations, helping businesses maintain compliance and mitigate risks.

	•	Company Information
This section allows users to input and maintain vital company details such as legal entity name, address, contact information, and organizational structure. It serves as the foundation for various ERP processes, ensuring accurate representation and identification of the company within the system.

Company Information
Overview Description:
The configuration for company information facilitates the input of essential company details, including Registered Name, Trading Name, Tax Number, Registration Number, Billing, and Shipping Address.
This entered information serves to automate the inclusion of company details on system-generated documents intended for customers, suppliers, or record-keeping purposes.

Tax Rules & Regulations
Overview Description:
The configuration for tax rules and regulations enables the creation of multiple tax classes, each designated for sellable products, assemblies, and items. These tax classes are comprised of several components, including Tax Rate, Collection Jurisdiction, Destination Jurisdiction, and the effective start date.
Below are the definitions for each component:
Collection Jurisdiction
	•	Definition: The specific location from which the sales transaction originates, typically representing the seller's business premises or the point of dispatch for the goods.
	•	Determining Factor: The seller's business address or the site from which the products are shipped.
Destination Jurisdiction
	•	Definition: The location where the goods are ultimately delivered, typically corresponding to the buyer's location.
	•	Determining Factor: The delivery address or the buyer's business location where the goods are received.
Tax Rate
	•	The tax rate is the VAT or sales tax in which you charge the buyer.
Start Date
	•	Current Date: If you are setting up the tax class to be used immediately, you can use the current date.
	•	Future Date: If the tax class will apply from a specific future date (e.g., the start of a new fiscal period or in anticipation of a tax rate change), you should set that future date.
	•	Historical Date: If you are entering the tax class to reflect a period that has already begun (e.g., backdating to align with fiscal policies or corrections), you should use the relevant past date.

HR and Training Overview
HR and Training Module Description
The HR and Training Module facilitates the management of employee or contractor information and records within the system.
Users can add employees or contractors as access users, granting them specific permissions to perform tasks within the ERP system. Alternatively, individuals can be added as non-access users for record-keeping purposes.
In summary, this module serves as a comprehensive tool for managing personnel and resources, whether for maintaining records or assigning permissions within the ERP system.
HR and Training Module Process Flow
￼
HR and Training Sub Modules
	•	User Management
The ArcFlow User Management Sub Module allows admin users to create users to be loaded onto the system with their allocated permissions.
You are able to create two types of users which are outlined below:
	◦	No Access User: User won’t need access to the platform.
	◦	Access User: User needs log in and access to the platform.
	•	Each type of user will have their own specified permissions and access to certain modules, sub modules and features when navigating and performing actions on the system.


User Management
Overview Description:
The ArcFlow User Management Sub Module allows admin users to create users to be loaded onto the system with their allocated permissions.
You are able to create two types of users which are outlined below:
Access User
Access Users require login credentials and access to the ERP platform. They have permissions assigned to them based on their role and responsibilities within the organization. These permissions dictate what actions they can perform within the system, such as viewing, creating, editing, or deleting data, based on the modules and features they need to access to fulfill their job duties.
No Access User
No Access Users do not require access or assigned roles and responsibilities within the ERP system. They are individuals involved in your business operations but do not need direct system access. While you can record, pay, and track these users and interact with them through the system, they do not need ERP access to carry out their daily tasks.
Each type of user will have their own specified permissions and access to certain modules, sub modules and features when navigating and performing actions on the system.

Blueprints Overview
Blueprints Module Description
This module is where the products, assemblies and items are managed. This encompasses their Bill of Materials (BOM), Routing and metadata.
The blueprints modules encompasses two sub modules being the blueprints library and the routing for associated products, assemblies and items.
The library is where the database of all items, assemblies and products are managed. This allows for users to go through and a host of information about each of the stored entities including their BOM, routing, metadata and explosions (list of every item in the entity).
The setup of the Blueprints library and routing processes allows for warehouse stock to be updated, sales processes to be established, procurement cycles and enables the production through manufactured routes.
BOM Process and Structure
A bill of materials (BOM) is a comprehensive list of all the components, parts, and raw materials required to produce a finished Assembly or Product. It includes detailed information about each item, such as the part number, description, quantity, and the relationship between the components. The BOM serves as a reference for production planning, inventory management, and cost estimation. It ensures that all the necessary materials are available and that the production process runs smoothly.
The BOM follows a structure as seen in the diagram below:
￼
Routing Processes and Structure
Routing refers to the defined sequence of operations or steps that need to be followed during the manufacturing or production process of a product or assembly. It outlines the specific tasks, workstations, and resources required at each step to transform the raw materials or components into a finished product. This can also include any documentation or quality controls required during a part of the process.
The routes of a BOM can follow two distinct processes being manufacturing routes and sub contracted routes.
The high level overview of the assembly or product route is found below and elaborated further on the “Routing” training folder:
￼
Blueprints Module Process Flow
￼
Blueprints Sub Modules
	•	Library
The library is where the database of all items, assemblies and products are stored. This allows for staff to go through and a host of information about each of the stored entities including their BOM, routing, metadata and explosions (list of every item in the entity).

	•	Routing
Routing refers to the defined sequence of operations or steps that need to be followed during the manufacturing or production process of a product or assembly. It outlines the specific tasks, workstations, and resources required at each step to transform the raw materials or components into a finished product. This can also include any documentation or quality controls required during a part of the process.

Library
Library Overview Description:
The Blueprints module facilitates the digital creation of your manufacturing company's Items, Assemblies, and Products.
This module allows you to meticulously define and create isolated items, assemblies, and products, each with their key information and attributes. These attributes seamlessly integrate into and support various processes regarding ordering, sales, manufacturing, and storage of the created items, assemblies and products.
Additionally, the Blueprints module facilitates the creation of Bill of Materials (BOM) structures for assemblies and products. This step is crucial as it establishes the foundation for the manufacturing routes needed to produce the specified structures.
By leveraging the Blueprints module, you ensure a cohesive and efficient workflow from the initial creation of components to the final production stages.
Definitions and Key Attributes
Item
An item stands as the fundamental building block, situated at the lowest level of the BOM hierarchy within assemblies or products. These items encompass raw materials or any components incapable of further subdivision into smaller parts.
The key attributes and their definitions are found below:
	•	Is Shipping Container
If you tag an item as “Is Shipping Container” the system will store this items as a container for packaging completed sellable stock for customer delivery. These items will be presented in the fulfilment module when you need to allocate packaging materials for customer deliveries. An example of this type of item will be a wooden pallet.

	•	Is Shipping Supplies
If you tag an Item as “Is Shipping Supplies” the system will store the item for the purposes of protecting sellable stock inside the shipping container. An example of this type of item would be bubble wrap.

	•	Is Sub Contracted
If you tag an Item as “Is Sub Contacted” it means that you will not be able to directly procure this item. Rather, you will have to create a sub contracted route that has this item as a result.

	•	Supplier Conversion
When you load an item you allocate your internal Unit of Measure. When you are linking the supplier which will supply a particular item, you enter in the suppliers UOM. If there is a difference between the conversion of your UOM to the suppliers UOM, please enter the conversion of the single supplier UOM compared to your UOM of the item. You can enter in "1" if there is an exact conversion between you and your supplier.
Eg:
Your UOM: Box Supplier's UOM: Carton Conversion rate: 1 Carton = 10 Boxes If you need to order 50 Boxes of screws from your supplier, you'll first need to convert it to their unit of measure:
50 Boxes * (1 Carton / 10 Boxes) = 5 Cartons
So, you would need to order 5 Cartons of screws from your supplier to fulfill your requirement of 50 Boxes.

	•	Can Sell
If you tag an Item as “Can Sell” it means that you can directly add the item as an individual line item on a quote or invoice. These items will need to be stored in the finished goods warehouse area type.

Assembly
An assembly consists of multiple child items and additional sub-assemblies. These components are combined into a Bill of Materials (BOM) to create the assembly. Physically, assemblies are produced through a sequence of operations defined in their production route. An assembly can also be included in the BOM of a parent assembly or final product.
The key attributes and their definitions are found below:
	•	Is Sub Contracted
If you tag an assembly as “Is Sub Contracted” it suggests that, although there is a Bill of Material for producing it in-house, the entire assembly will be manufactured by an external company.

	•	Is Phantom
A Phantom Assembly refers to a a group of components used temporarily in the production process. It is not a physical assembly, rather a virtual grouping of items for manufacturing convenience, bypassing inventory tracking.

	•	Is Manufactured In-House
If an assembly is tagged “Is Manufactured In-House” it suggests the assembly is produced in-house by following its routing process and associated BOM.

	•	Is Packaging
The Assembly created is used for packing purposes and not directly linked to the BOM structure of a parent assembly or final product.

	•	Can Sell
If you tag an Assembly as “Can Sell” it means that you can directly add the Assembly as an individual line item on a quote or invoice. These Assemblies will need to be stored in the finished goods warehouse area type.

Product
A product is the highest level in a Bill of Materials (BOM) structure. It is a collection of items and assemblies, created through a BOM. Unlike assemblies or items, a product cannot be included as a child in another BOM structure. Physically, products are produced through a sequence of operations outlined in their routing process. Products are typically ordered by customers and manufactured specifically for sales.
The key attributes and their definitions are found below:
	•	Is Sub Contracted
If you tag a Product as “Is Sub Contracted” it suggests that, although there is a Bill of Material for producing it in-house, the entire Product will be manufactured by an external company.

	•	Is Packaging
The product and BOM is used for packaging purposes for the delivery of additional sellable products.

	•	Is Manufactured In-House
If a Product is tagged “Is Manufactured In-House” it suggests the Product is produced in-house by following its routing process and associated BOM.

	•	Can Sell
If you tag a Product as “Can Sell” it means that you can directly add the Product as an individual line item on a quote or invoice. These Products will need to be stored in the finished goods warehouse area type.

BOM Structure:
￼
Enabling of External Workflows
Routing
Once you have completed your library and BOM structures, you can create manufacturing or subcontracting routes for items, assemblies, and products. The routes are made up of processes associated with the BOM.
Sales
Once you have completed your library, you are able to add the items, assemblies or products onto sales quotes and invoices. Additionally, sales orders will be created which will feed production processes.
Procurement
Once you have completed your library, you are able to request quotes from suppliers for the created items, assemblies and products which then convert to purchase orders and received ordered items will be assigned to the warehouses.
Warehouse Stock
The creation of the products, assemblies and items also allows you to add stock values into the warehouse for the created products, assemblies and items.
Production
Created items, assemblies and products and their associated BOM and routes feed into the production processes through the completion of processes based on its route.

22\. The minimum re-order quantity is minimum amount that can be ordered at one time. This avoids the situation where you only purchase one screw when you are one short instead of buying a bag.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/d59a3603-af99-4542-8aef-0a77f42195db/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,204&br_px=859,685&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=392,212
23\. The minimum stock quantity is the stock level at which the a.i will begin to alert the user to procure more of said item.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/421c9267-6ae1-4e7c-a277-a4d5ec9510d1/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1162,190&br_px=2022,671&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
24\. The last paid unit price is used to create estimations for the cost during procurement. This will then change to the last paid unit price once the system is fully functioning.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/0b6f63ce-ac0b-40d8-8b2b-253e0c29e0f1/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=68,109&br_px=1444,878&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=524,277
25\. Average unit price is used if the user knows the average price paid but not the last paid unit price.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/0cc262aa-060f-41a4-ab48-35665ce80f17/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1072,252&br_px=1932,733&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
26\. The ordering description can be used to add any extra information which may be necessary during the procurement phase such as special requests for the supplier.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/a9eb5be8-eaac-4d4b-9791-c3dfb265740a/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=76,298&br_px=1223,939&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=523,277
27\. If you mark this item as a sellable item- this means that the sales team will be able to sell it on to a customer even though it was not a manufactured product. You will then need to indicate how many you want in stock ready to be sold.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/9e362edd-0ad5-4a45-8ad4-9eb61a66f843/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,575&br_px=859,1056&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=216,212
28\. Avg Monthly Sales is used by the system to estimate how many you will need in a given month and will alert procurement when it estimates you are running low.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/5602a13b-98d1-4b7e-9d20-d4dc29e1faa3/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1050,505&br_px=2197,1146&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=523,277
29\. The unit price is the price at which the sales staff sell the item on to the customer.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/e837f02d-7b4f-4c73-a675-af83b1a19d00/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1109,681&br_px=1969,1162&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
30\. We can also add price breaks directly to this item. This will be visible for the sales staff.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/0b538189-8901-47a9-9f76-8e22c43b1608/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,724&br_px=859,1205&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=141,212
31\. Click this field.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/95b9b920-614e-4ada-8981-dd72ccd97246/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,736&br_px=859,1217&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=145,212
32\. Here we can add the weight of the item which will be used during the shipping step to calculate shipping costs.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/1b6c53ce-b63c-458e-8b88-3a76658d63f8/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,641&br_px=1719,1602&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=468,276
33\. The dimensions can also be entered for the shipping.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/0f5659cd-bb36-4a3f-87a8-6cdd203a57d7/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1087,877&br_px=1947,1358&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
34\. The tax class for this item can be selected from the drop down.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/cb43d439-719d-4dfc-88ea-e71534d0fb41/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=86,966&br_px=945,1447&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
35\. If you offer your customers a warranty on this item you can then assign this warranty type here.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/30c37010-18ba-4fdc-8ef2-22737710d782/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1138,1122&br_px=1998,1603&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
36\. The 'Track by Batch" and "Track by Serial" buttons allow you to opt for this item to be tracked by your own internal batch or serial number.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/94e778d3-19cd-4afd-a1c5-fa768ed0b26b/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,1073&br_px=859,1554&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=101,212
37\. Lets move to the Manufacturer tab.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/126a3c94-205a-40e9-bb1b-9aea10210e3b/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=92,0&br_px=951,480&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,200
38\. We can select the manufacturer from the drop down. By associating the manufacturer with the item we can then input its manufacturers part number which can be used during procurement.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/9ebac417-2411-4a47-95a2-ad7030880289/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,180&br_px=859,661&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=197,212
39\. We input the Manufacturers Part number.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/473f5fb8-0e36-4f30-9c06-d8b76d887350/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=24,189&br_px=883,670&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
40\. We also indicate what type of carrier the manufacturer uses. An example of a carrier is resistors which are carried in a reel.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/041bb4af-d871-4647-a9f5-0794d80cca28/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=664,297&br_px=1524,778&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
41\. We indicate the capacity of this carrier so that we know the max amount that can be ordered in each carrier.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/f0ca16f2-1a93-4c63-a4d4-0b8ee6d021f4/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1418,183&br_px=2278,664&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
42\. In the Documents section we can store any files which may be of relevance to the item. An example would be the design tolerances for a bolt or the info sheet for an electrical part.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/a3345ff1-392d-4d4b-95cb-dc438080ff7b/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=254,0&br_px=1114,480&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,205
Made with Scribe

	•	Edit and View an Item
Step 1: Select the "Library"
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/b1be3787-406e-4f6f-a4ce-5a0c78dd4dc4/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,0&br_px=2293,1281&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=280,274
Step 2: Select the "Items" tab.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/ddbe6abb-c3d9-4689-b833-14a7b3b310ca/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,53&br_px=2293,1334&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=404,277
Step 3: A global list of all previously created items will be listed. You can select the specific item in which you would like to edit or view.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/eacee71c-1e30-47c2-9b31-074b59d588f9/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,63&br_px=3439,1986&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=219,371
Step 4: You can now view and edit any previously created details of the item. First you can view the general information.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/0bb9604a-15c9-4a58-8c6d-69643cc2f401/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,0&br_px=3439,1922&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=145,130
If you select the suppliers tab, you can remove or add suppliers of the item and create new supplier conversions which will be utilised at procurement.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/bc97658f-700b-4858-ac73-6dd7579d1f85/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,0&br_px=2293,1281&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=328,207
The ordering and sales tab allows you to view and edit the information regarding ordering and selling of the item.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/36b447f8-860a-4d56-8847-d5c30b45dc17/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,0&br_px=2293,1281&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=458,202
You are able to link manufacturers to the item for quality control and tracking purposes.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/94df4940-c7dc-4252-b263-005d2456d145/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,0&br_px=3439,1922&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=392,121
The associations tab will link all the direct parent assemblies or products in which the item has been linked to. You are able to de link the items here.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/b2221e3f-2cd1-4029-88b4-e50dab75251a/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=453,0&br_px=2746,1281&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=524,205
The document tab will display are uploaded documents.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/7b5b36fd-851a-4f07-b236-730aba87ba7f/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=16,0&br_px=3456,1922&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=548,122
The KPI metric tab will display the Key Performance Indicators for each different supplier which suppliers the item. The KPI will allow you to assess which supplier is most suitable for the supply of the items.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/ca02da93-3dcd-436d-8b2b-a93024e1b019/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,0&br_px=3439,1922&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=61,123

	•	Create an Assembly
1\. Start by entering in the internal code for the assembly.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/55ac85a1-5b97-46dc-affa-07e905206433/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,55&br_px=859,536&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=207,212
2\. Add the name of the assembly.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/1421afc8-8726-4b91-8911-bd24d71afbe0/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1093,68&br_px=1953,549&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
3\. Input the version of this assembly you are currently building if you use version control.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/d458db94-5328-4729-a9c0-fc3e0cebdcfe/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=106,117&br_px=966,598&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
4\. If this version has a revision number it can then be added here.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/783d7a52-09f5-446d-a49b-4bda229965fc/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=55,38&br_px=1432,807&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=524,277
5\. We can set the status of this assembly as active or inactive.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/a39f80e8-3bfb-4a27-b128-3a23f7021ebc/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1115,166&br_px=1975,647&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
6\. Set the unit of measure for this assembly.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/8ebd6603-7e32-4de9-8326-ae61adc09bc9/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1100,294&br_px=1960,775&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
7\. The assembly can be allocated to a category.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/ed81f295-86a1-4d9b-a41b-ba6b943abd23/user_cropped_screenshot.jpeg?tl_px=95,0&br_px=1472,412&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=564,84
8\. A sub-category can also be assigned for added granularity.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/a5878289-6dc8-410c-977d-183314acb2f0/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1159,401&br_px=2019,882&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
9\. We now move on to the Bill of Materials (BOM) tab. Here we will construct the structure of the assembly.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/7e8b458a-e73e-43bd-9562-4ab8c240b19a/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,0&br_px=859,480&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=252,205
10\. Using the items drop down we can allocate any items which make up this assembly. As we select each item we will see it populate below the assembly
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/29998235-8c29-4cef-bd00-fb75ac7108c2/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,105&br_px=859,586&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=174,212
11\. Im going to select a nut, washer and spacer.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/b9ce3d41-4f64-4340-a399-4b21628e6382/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,111&br_px=859,592&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=280,212
12\. You can then adjust the quantity of each line item using the numerical input boxes highlighted in orange. If you use a designator for the line item during manufacturing this can be allocated in the box highlighted in red.

26\. You then need to move onto the ordering and selling tab.

27\. This field sets the minimum amount of this assembly you can should be able to make from your stock at any time. If the system sees you are running low on a raw material needed to manufacture this assembly it will alert procurement.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/db5ced41-1847-4acb-9eb6-ae9be130a4ae/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,127&br_px=859,608&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=317,212

31\.

	•	Edit and View an Assembly
Step 1: Select "Library"
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/4fd8c9ed-2150-4292-9271-f3e442fa0f9f/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,0&br_px=2293,1281&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=280,276
Step 2: Select the Assemblies tab.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/36cb9e3d-1cd4-493a-a0ae-44736f81382d/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,211&br_px=1719,1172&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=374,277
Step 3: A global list of all previously created assemblies will be listed. You can select the specific assembly in which you want to view or edit.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/aa15b15c-65b5-48a1-8ca2-a80d71240a42/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,63&br_px=3439,1986&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=220,364
Step 4: You can work through each tab to view and edit the information. The general tab allows you to view and edit the assemblies basic information.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/27a05184-ac6e-406f-8119-90c67b76aaff/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,0&br_px=2293,1281&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=256,175
The BOM tab allow you to view the assemblies BOM structure and add or remove further children to its structure.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/cb303801-4b30-4ad5-847b-1f35e0c905b1/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,0&br_px=3439,1922&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=252,106
The explosion tab lists all the individual child items and their associated quantities linked to the assembly.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/30d2a7b4-413f-4e7f-9536-ac5185d92e67/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=11,0&br_px=2304,1281&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=524,174
The manufacturing tab allows you to change the manufacturing attributes such as the assembly being sub contracted or manufactured in hour.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/e8799022-d559-47b4-8c0d-95ffa91be0f4/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,0&br_px=3439,1922&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=433,104
The ordering and selling tab allows you to edit and view the ordering quantities, costing based on component and labour costs. You are able to manually add the costs or over our time, the system will recommend the accurate costing. You are able to tag if the assembly is sellable or if it is just a child to another sellable parent product or assembly.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/b1cccc3d-45fb-4a35-b17f-c39d343c943f/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=8,0&br_px=3448,1922&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=524,107
The association tab will list all of the parent products, assemblies or child assembly or items in which the assembly is linked to through alternative BOM structures.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/ba3d5e8b-fb61-4adf-92a4-4e8b77084d9a/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=16,0&br_px=3456,1922&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=601,107

	•	Create a Product
1\. We start by entering in the internal Product code.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/eaf88391-cc1c-46d2-8550-06bff42280cc/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,59&br_px=859,540&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=334,212
2\. The internal product name is entered here.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/16ec9342-6863-48c2-bbef-d208f5e19eca/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1361,68&br_px=2221,549&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
3\. If the product is tracked by version it can be selected and the version can be input.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/0ac25c86-5602-4b14-b27c-5f6b313fb59f/user_cropped_screenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,0&br_px=1581,782&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=819,205
4\. If the product is tracked by its revision it can be selected and the revision number can be added.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/4bdd5019-d56a-40f7-a96e-93a13af74082/user_cropped_screenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,0&br_px=1577,862&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=709,267
5\. The unit of measure for the product is selected.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/afb8e11a-729e-49fb-9ed2-0322d828f005/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1159,303&br_px=2019,784&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
6\. The product is set to either an active or inactive status.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/a8b8fd0b-12d4-4145-9693-6b8954f313f2/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1111,172&br_px=1971,653&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
7\. The product can be classified to a category.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/7140ce43-f205-4aa9-a52f-89d9f0acea4d/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=12,90&br_px=1731,1051&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=524,277
8\. It can be further classified using the sub-category.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/35540a5f-425c-4ebd-9c83-1e13e6b6d1ee/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1140,368&br_px=2000,849&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
9\. We can now build the Bill of Material for this product.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/a97f469c-5036-4a02-a3bd-a84ec21782e0/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,0&br_px=859,480&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=249,206
10\. Using the drop down we can select all the items which form part of this product. These are selected using the tick boxes and their quantities can be altered when they are inside the product structure.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/e42760e3-c91c-4498-bb4c-cdaa80029fe7/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,268&br_px=859,749&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=121,212
11\. Using this dropdown we can select all the sub-assemblies which form part of this product. These are selected using the tick boxes and their quantities can be altered when they are inside the product structure.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/67baeecd-4d23-491b-896b-5c9389ac7ed3/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,225&br_px=859,706&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=361,212
12\. Here we can see an example of a product which has been alloacted 2 assemblies and 3 items.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/b8194659-6151-41f2-8619-e26f91aabaec/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,144&br_px=1376,913&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=92,277
13\. The quantities of a selected item or assembly can be altered inside the product structure.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/d82fc067-dd1a-4638-a7ba-9dc5754cba24/user_cropped_screenshot.jpeg?tl_px=139,0&br_px=1859,813&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=901,223
14\. If we are satisfied with the BOM structure we can move onto the manufacturing settings.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/170091be-0468-4905-bdd2-0eca61e38188/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,0&br_px=859,480&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=365,190
15\. If the product is sub-contracted out for full or partial assembly you will select this option.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/4484635f-fe9a-4b98-9587-384e871e7aa5/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,112&br_px=859,593&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=99,212
16\. A phantom product simplifies manufacturing by combining multiple components into one virtual product. If that is the case then select this option.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/7933869e-4e19-4309-8449-061d4444762e/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,145&br_px=859,626&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=101,212
17\. If this product is manufactured in house then select this option.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/178e66eb-2653-46b5-b839-50855994f0a0/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1037,110&br_px=1897,591&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
18\. Select this if the product is going to be used as a packaging material then select
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/90c60ceb-07d6-462c-bccf-5dc5dfaae119/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1030,148&br_px=1890,629&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
19\. The Minimum Manufacturable Batch is the smallest batch size you can manufacture.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/20ec776d-639a-4cab-947b-9a7316b04e7b/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,199&br_px=859,680&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=220,212
20\. The Maximum Manufacturable Batch is the smallest batch size you can manufacture.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/80946b18-349c-4e11-a8b6-960db4c73367/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1170,194&br_px=2030,675&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
21\. The User Average Build Duration is an estimate of how long it would take to build this product. Once the system has tracked the product through its manufacturing process it will calcualte this.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/f73856fa-033d-4c68-b50f-7acd2101d7e7/user_cropped_screenshot.jpeg?tl_px=78,0&br_px=1454,546&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=719,246
22\. Selecting this option will allow the system to track this product using a batch number system.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/04d9e3b2-1a47-43ee-bde3-abb850e0a59a/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,355&br_px=859,836&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=104,212
23\. You will need to set the batch prefix.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/9f0beff5-4b91-475a-b95c-5ba375579dda/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,404&br_px=859,885&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=152,212
24\. Selecting this option will allow the system to track this product using a serial number system.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/9aee86ca-4db3-4508-8d78-1c880c175807/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1037,352&br_px=1897,833&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
25\. You will need to set the serial prefix.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/4387f305-92fd-499e-8766-a51dd4075726/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1057,408&br_px=1917,889&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
26\. Lets move onto the Ordering & Selling tab.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/a12b6320-4111-4154-ba46-e3dcfdb6dd46/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=77,0&br_px=936,480&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,198
27\. The Minimum Production Capacity from Raw Material Stock sets the minimum amount of this product you should be able to manufacture from the current stock levels of its items and assemblies. The system will use this number to ensure there is always a suitable amount of components to make up this product.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/879e755a-d23e-4e7e-aed4-2da6215e7e9a/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,136&br_px=859,617&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=315,212
28\. Here you enter the dimensions of the product for shipping consideration.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/4a0e5636-e67b-4aef-885e-d411e1aa7d8a/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1068,121&br_px=1928,602&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
29\. In the costing section the user will need to provide estimates of the labour and operations cost so the system has an initial value to use for its cost estimates. Once the system has run through the manufacture of this product it will then calcualte accurate costing.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/2337b11d-5d35-4898-906e-e1ace9fa9a86/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=66,194&br_px=1213,835&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=524,277
30\. The user will need to provide a Bill of Materials cost. This can either be an estimate or it can just be copied from the material costs calculated by the system.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/ac9c88c0-c8f4-42de-94ea-532cc21e84e6/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=65,388&br_px=925,869&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
31\.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/eb0d9171-c82a-4f82-b542-fed1d3d7f173/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1008,388&br_px=1868,869&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
32\. If the 'Can Sell' button is clicked this product will be available to be sold to your customers.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/1bb23a6a-4afc-455c-a43d-45abb460aedb/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,521&br_px=859,1002&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=103,212
33\. The Minimum Finished Goods Quantity in Stock tells the system how many of the product you should have available at anytime and will action manufacturing if the stock level is below the set amount.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/635e1cc5-eace-4b7a-a244-9c48ba15852a/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,575&br_px=859,1056&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=219,212
34\. The Average Monthly Sales is an estimate provided by the user so the system can begin to forecast demand for this product. This is before it has begun collecting data from real sales through the ERP.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/05399679-7750-470d-ad48-63b4732169bb/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1315,579&br_px=2175,1060&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
35\. Click this text field.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/5b32d007-727a-4ff3-b943-d19a402df9ec/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=4,819&br_px=863,1300&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212
36\. The dimensions for the finished product are input here for shipping calculations.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-07/152fb428-f2f0-4328-9e6b-d28e7b8d1952/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1106,809&br_px=1966,1290&force_format=png&width=860&wat_scale=76&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=402,212

!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-08/15ff37c7-7578-43db-948a-3b2d3adc90b3/user_cropped_screenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,0&br_px=1559,769&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=790,268

	•	Edit and View a Product
Step 1: Select "Library"
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/e6191fa7-f344-4222-ad95-99336ddc3c82/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,1&br_px=2293,1282&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=292,277
Step 2: Select the Products tab. A global list of all previously created assemblies will be listed. You can select the specific assembly in which you want to view or edit.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/e34302fc-5a4d-4f49-8bee-c531fda7f5b6/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,529&br_px=1719,1490&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=443,276
Step 3: You can work through each tab to view and edit the information. The general tab allows you to view and edit the products basic information.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/2c090e4c-504a-40de-8e6d-835a48abf4d8/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,0&br_px=2293,1281&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=266,200
The BOM tab allow you to view the products BOM structure and add or remove further children to its structure.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/a4b77326-143b-4507-a65f-4c3e4f4ce8d5/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,0&br_px=2293,1281&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=380,201
The explosion tab lists all the individual child items and their associated quantities linked to the product.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/2ba5a971-3845-447a-a752-f003dc11f6d0/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,0&br_px=2293,1281&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=516,198
The manufacturing tab allows you to change the manufacturing attributes such as the assembly being sub contracted or manufactured in house.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/19fe704a-cf69-48d2-b4cd-2f6605747d9c/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,0&br_px=3439,1922&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=426,119
The ordering and selling tab allows you to edit and view the ordering quantities, costing based on component and labour costs. You are able to manually add the costs or over our time, the system will recommend the accurate costing. You are able to tag if the product is sellable.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-31/c3b567f3-973a-48ff-b260-d4430ea0472c/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=16,0&br_px=3456,1922&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=531,119
The association tab will list all of the linked child assemblies and items.

Routing
Overview Description:
The ArcFlow routing functionality is essential for planning and sequencing the operations needed to transform raw materials or components into finished assemblies and products.
These established routes integrate with your internal production processes to create and schedule job cards for completing the associated tasks. Additionally, subcontracted routes can be set up to outsource the manufacturing of items, assemblies, or products.
This routing forms the foundation of production scheduling, planning, and capacity management.
The ArcFlow system allows you to create routing for the following processes:
Manufactured Assembly Routes
Manufactured Assembly Routes consist of a series of operations carried out through your internal manufacturing processes to produce an assembly. These routes utilize the Bill of Materials (BOM) structure, which comprise of children items and assemblies, and involve various processes performed by your employees at designated workstations.
Prerequisites:
	•	The Assembly needs to be tagged with “Is Manufactured In-House”
	•	The Assembly needs a BOM Structure
	•	If there are children Assemblies part of the BOM structure, they needs to have an already established route.
Manufactured Product Routes
Manufactured Product Routes consist of a series of operations carried out through your internal manufacturing processes to produce a Product. These routes utilize the Bill of Materials (BOM) structure, which comprise of children items and assemblies, and involve various processes performed by your employees at designated workstations.
Prerequisites:
	•	The Product needs to be tagged with “Is Manufactured In-House”
	•	The Product needs a BOM Structure
	•	If there are children Assemblies part of the BOM structure, they needs to have an already established route.
Sub Contracted Routes
Subcontracted routes can be created for items, assemblies, and products that are not processed in-house. For items, subcontracted routes are necessary when direct procurement is not possible, requiring the item to be obtained through an external manufacturing process. For assemblies and products, even though there is a Bill of Materials for in-house production, subcontracted routes mean the entire assembly or product will be manufactured by an external company.
Prerequisites:
	•	The item, assembly or product needs to be tagged with “Is Sub Contracted”
	•	You need to have created Sub Contractor services suppliers in the procurement module
Assembly and Product Manufactured Route Definitions
Each routing process comprises the following key workflows:
	•	Input: This encompasses the items or assemblies required for the process, which can either be the output from the preceding completed process or externally sourced materials.
	•	Process: This stage entails the specific operations, instructions, and tools necessary to execute the task or process outlined in the input stage.
	•	Output: The output represents the end results of the processed input, which subsequently form the final output of the process and are transferred to the subsequent process as inputs.
The routing process is intricately linked to the assembly or product Bill of Materials (BOM). Moreover, each step within the routing process is associated with a designated workstation and assigned employees responsible for its execution.
The final step of the routing process of an assembly or product is linked to a warehouse type storing the partial or final form of the completed assembly or product.
Functioning as a comprehensive roadmap for the entire production process, the routing ensures seamless guidance for every work order, operation, and assembly step, thereby facilitating the timely and efficient completion of the final product.
Additionally, the routing serves as the cornerstone for capacity planning activities once job cards have been assigned, aiding in the optimization of production resources and schedules.
Sub Contracted Route Definitions
The sub contracted routes comprises of utilising a sub contractor, which was created in the procurement module, to outsource the manufacturing processes.
Each route comprises of the following key terms:
	•	Sub Contractor: A type of servicing suppliers which receives your sent items, assemblies or products and completes their own internal route prior to convert the received stock into a finished state.
	•	Sent to Sub Contractor: The items, assemblies or products sent to the sub contractor to be converted into its finished state.
	•	Instructions: A set of document instructions which outline the request of work performance and details to convert the received items, assemblies or products into its finished state.
	•	Received from Sub Contractor: The outsourced manufactured items, assemblies or products which have been processed through your set of instructions into the finished state.
Since the route is sub contracted, you will utilise the procurement module to generate a RFQ and Purchase Order prior to the route being established. Once the route has been completed, you will receive the item, assembly or product in its finished state and allocate them to the correct warehouse.

	•	Create Manufacturing Assembly Route

!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-06-02/302469d0-19e8-4f1b-8a9e-509427499bdf/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,63&br_px=3439,1986&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=245,386

You can enter in the state in which the process ends.

	•	Create Manufacturing Product Route
The following product route has been created to follow a two step process. The first step is to assemble the product and then the second step is to quality control the product. The product is then placed in the finished good store.
During the walkthrough you will note the input, process and output needed at each stage of the process within the route.
Step 1: Select the "Routing" Sub Module
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-30/a68eb85b-e07f-4e94-bd16-6705accd07c5/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=233,0&br_px=2526,1281&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=523,267
Step 2: Select a product which you will aim to create a route for.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-30/f9c7306f-f0da-4268-8b30-654742a31111/user_cropped_screenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,63&br_px=3439,1986&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=119,277
Step 3: You will now use our visual process flow builder by select the "Create Process" button.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-30/207ef738-a375-48cb-8ec8-0a051f3e18d3/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=16,0&br_px=3456,1922&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=873,121
Step 4: Type in the process name and link the process to the associated workstation where the process will be performed.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-30/c3a8cdfa-e949-4d4f-ab75-8e898c71ef23/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=319,417&br_px=2612,1698&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=523,277
The drop down list will provide you with a list of possible workstations.

Step 5: Select the "Create" button to add the newly created process.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-30/ee7046c7-d204-46ae-9c33-8df3abf77bf5/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=962,767&br_px=2682,1728&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=524,276
Step 6: Repeat the process outlined in step 5 to create a new process which will be linked to the product.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-30/a79a956f-7010-42eb-a1d6-eed0532a008c/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=16,0&br_px=3456,1922&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=869,123

Step 7: Place you cursor to the edge of the start block to initiate the route. You will drag the cursor to the next connecting process in the route.

Step 8: Every product route needs to be completed through the placement of the product to the associated warehouse. Since it is a product, we will add a "Finished Goods" warehouse as the final destination.

Step 9: You will now connect the final process to the associated warehouse.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-30/d317ac60-be8d-4fd6-b782-fa60ad985d14/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=1051,597&br_px=3344,1878&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=524,277
Step 10: You have now created the process flow and high level processes which form part of the route. You will need to define the Input, Process and Output which will occur at each newly created process.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-30/43159395-5dd9-4c8b-a1da-ab4c3ac540f0/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=0,0&br_px=3439,1922&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=234,59
Step 11: Since we created the first process to assemble the product, we need to define the input or what is received at this process. We will add the entire BOM structure as it is needed to assemble.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-30/6ed8e93c-ca62-40ea-8684-c862f6ea724e/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=16,32&br_px=3456,1955&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=791,277

Step 12: We now need to define the process. The process is the action that happens to the input to transform it to an output. You are able to add tools, templates and instructions.
!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-30/58f11dfe-2368-4b73-a6b3-962d8bc209a7/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=16,18&br_px=3456,1941&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=745,277

Step 13: You now need to define the output based on the processing of the input.

!https://ajeuwbhvhr.cloudimg.io/colony-recorder.s3.amazonaws.com/files/2024-05-30/ce203b40-3098-457f-8c1d-14b15ca2d568/ascreenshot.jpeg?tl_px=16,63&br_px=3456,1986&force_format=png&width=1120.0&wat=1&wat_opacity=0.7&wat_gravity=northwest&wat_url=https://colony-recorder.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/images/watermarks/FB923C_standard.png&wat_pad=781,548
